= V4 Outline MultiLine NoSorting TabWidth=30

H="Project Outline"
/* 
********************HEADING******************** 

Project Name: JAMA figure for Sean

Outline:  
Per Amy's instructions on 10/16/19, Sean would like to look at a cross-sectional graph of Medicare recipients by age and illness.

Because this is a very quick project, we'll use the NHATS ICD-9/10 final data but include the updated CCW codes as well.


Date Started: 10/17/19

Primary Investigator: Sean Morrison
Funding Source: 

Created by: EBL

Primary Analyst: EBL
Secondary Analyst: 

Datasets Used: nhats, nhats-linked Medicare claims only for full death info





H="pull index from ICD-9/10 data"


H="get chronic conditions using correct CCW algorithm"
//get chronic condition indicators using actual CCW methodology

/*
Basic Structure
-look back over a certain time frame (1-3 years, depending on the condition) some 
 distance away from an already spidentified index date
-pull the dx codes separately for each relevant claim type and period for each condition
*/


/*First, make smaller versions of each claim type by matching only to sample and 
keeping only spid, index date, admit date, and diagnoses*/

use "D:\NHATS\Projects\serious_illness\ask_identifying_serious_illness_icd9_to_10\data\final_data\serious_ill_nhats_1_6_full_6m.dta" if wave==5 & sp_ivw==1 & nhres==0 & lml==0, clear
keep spid bene_id index_date wave


tempfile index
save `index'

use "D:\NHATS\Shared\base_data\CMS_claims\Stata\ip_06_17.dta", clear
rename icd_dgns_cd* dgnscd*
	
tempfile ip
save `ip'

foreach type in op pb hh snf dm hs {
	use `index', clear
	
	merge 1:m bene_id using "D:\NHATS\Shared\base_data\CMS_claims\Stata/`type'_09_17.dta", keep(match) nogen
	rename icd_dgns_cd* dgnscd*
	tempfile `type'
	save ``type''
}

foreach type in ip op pb hh snf dm hs {
	use bene_id admit_date dgnscd* using ``type'', clear
	merge m:1 bene_id using `index', keep(match using) nogen
	gen clmnum=_n

	forvalues i=1/3 {
		preserve
		keep if inrange(admit_date,index_date-floor(`i'*365.25),index_date-floor((`i'-1)*365.25))
		reshape long dgnscd, i(clmnum) j(num)
		drop if missing(dgnscd)
		duplicates drop spid clmnum dgnscd, force
		tempfile `type'`i'
		save ``type'`i''
		restore
}
	use ``type'1', clear
	forvalues i=2/3 {
		append using ``type'`i''
}
	tempfile `type'
	save ``type''
}

//3rd, get condition codes

use `index', clear
foreach year in 1 {

/*Acquired Hypothyroidism
-1 year look back
-1 IP/SNF/HH or 2 OP/PB
-any dx
*/


preserve


use `ip' if inrange(admit_date,index_date-floor(`year'*365.25),index_date-floor((`year'-1)*365.25)), clear
append using `snf'
append using `hh'
keep if inrange(admit_date,index_date-floor(`year'*365.25),index_date-floor((`year'-1)*365.25))
gen ccw1=`ccw1'
by spid, sort: egen ccw1a=max(ccw1)
keep spid ccw1a
duplicates drop
tempfile t1
save `t1'


use `pb' if inrange(admit_date,index_date-floor(`year'*365.25),index_date-floor((`year'-1)*365.25)), clear
append using `op'
keep if inrange(admit_date,index_date-floor(`year'*365.25),index_date-floor((`year'-1)*365.25))

gen ccw1=`ccw1'

by spid, sort: egen n_ccw1=total(ccw1)
gen ccw1b=n_ccw1>=2 & !missing(n_ccw1)
keep spid ccw1b
duplicates drop

merge 1:1 spid using `t1', nogen
egen ccw_1_y`year'=rowmax(ccw1*)
drop ccw1*
tempfile t2
save `t2'

restore

merge 1:1 spid using `t2', nogen
label var ccw_1_y`year' "Acquired Hypothyroidism, CCW, `=`year'-1'-`year' year pre-death"

/*AMI
-1 year look back
-1 IP
-dx 1 or 2 only
*/


preserve


use `ip' if inrange(admit_date,index_date-floor(`year'*365.25),index_date-floor((`year'-1)*365.25)), clear
keep if num<3
gen ccw2=`ccw2'
by spid, sort: egen ccw_2_y`year'=max(ccw2)
keep spid ccw_2_y`year'
duplicates drop
tempfile t1
save `t1'

restore

merge 1:1 spid using `t1', nogen

label var ccw_2_y`year' "AMI, CCW, `=`year'-1'-`year' year pre-death"

/*Alzheimer's
-3 year look back
-1 IP/SNF/HH/OP/PB
-any dx
*/

di "CCW 3"
di "year `year'"

preserve


use `pb' if inrange(admit_date,index_date-floor((`year'+2)*365.25),index_date-floor((`year'-1)*365.25)), clear
append using `ip'
append using `op'
append using `snf'
append using `hh'
keep if inrange(admit_date,index_date-floor((`year'+2)*365.25),index_date-floor((`year'-1)*365.25))
gen ccw3=`ccw3'
by spid, sort: egen ccw_3_y`year'=max(ccw3)
keep spid ccw_3_y`year'
duplicates drop
tempfile t1
save `t1'

restore

merge 1:1 spid using `t1', nogen

label var ccw_3_y`year' "Alzheimer's, CCW, `=`year'-1'-`year' year pre-death"


/*Alzheimer's Disease & Related Disorders or Senile Dementia

use `pb' if inrange(admit_date,index_date-floor(`year'*365.25),index_date-floor((`year'-1)*365.25)), clear
append using `op'
keep if inrange(admit_date,index_date-floor(`year'*365.25),index_date-floor((`year'-1)*365.25))

gen ccw11=`ccw11'

by spid, sort: egen n_ccw11=total(ccw11)
gen ccw11b=n_ccw11>=2 & !missing(n_ccw11)
keep spid ccw11b
duplicates drop

merge 1:1 spid using `t1', nogen
egen ccw_11_y`year'=rowmax(ccw11*)
drop ccw11*
tempfile t2
save `t2'

restore

merge 1:1 spid using `t2', nogen

label var ccw_11_y`year' "COPD/Bronchiectasis, CCW, `=`year'-1'-`year' year pre-death"

replace ccw22=0 if (substr(dgnscd,1,3)=="V57" | substr(dgnscd,1,5)=="Z5189") & num==1


by spid, sort: egen n_ccw22=total(ccw22)
gen ccw22b=n_ccw22>=2 & !missing(n_ccw22)
keep spid ccw22b
duplicates drop

merge 1:1 spid using `t1', nogen
egen ccw_22_y`year'=rowmax(ccw22*)
drop ccw22*
tempfile t2
save `t2'

restore

merge 1:1 spid using `t2', nogen

label var ccw_22_y`year' "Stroke/TIA, CCW, `=`year'-1'-`year' year pre-death"

/*Female/Male Breast Cancer		
-1 year look back
-1 IP/SNF/HH or 2 OP/PB
-any dx
*/


preserve


use `ip' if inrange(admit_date,index_date-floor(`year'*365.25),index_date-floor((`year'-1)*365.25)), clear
append using `snf'
append using `hh'
keep if inrange(admit_date,index_date-floor(`year'*365.25),index_date-floor((`year'-1)*365.25))
gen ccw23=`ccw23'

by spid, sort: egen ccw23a=max(ccw23)
keep spid ccw23a
duplicates drop
tempfile t1
save `t1'


use `pb' if inrange(admit_date,index_date-floor(`year'*365.25),index_date-floor((`year'-1)*365.25)), clear
append using `op'
keep if inrange(admit_date,index_date-floor(`year'*365.25),index_date-floor((`year'-1)*365.25))

gen ccw23=`ccw23'

by spid, sort: egen n_ccw23=total(ccw23)
gen ccw23b=n_ccw23>=2 & !missing(n_ccw23)
keep spid ccw23b
duplicates drop

merge 1:1 spid using `t1', nogen
egen ccw_23_y`year'=rowmax(ccw23*)
drop ccw23*
tempfile t2
save `t2'

restore

merge 1:1 spid using `t2', nogen

label var ccw_23_y`year' "F/M Breast Cancer, CCW, `=`year'-1'-`year' year pre-death"

forvalues i=1/27 {
	replace ccw_`i'_y`year'=0 if missing(ccw_`i'_y`year')
}


egen ccw_index_y`year'=rowtotal(ccw*y`year')
replace ccw_index_y`year'=ccw_index_y`year'-ccw_3_y`year'
label var ccw_index_y`year' "Index of conditions (excluding Alz for double-counting) `=`year'-1'-`year'"

gen ccw_ge3_y`year'=ccw_index_y`year'>=3
label var ccw_ge3_y`year' "3+ chronic conditions `=`year'-1'-`year'"

gen ccw_ge4_y`year'=ccw_index_y`year'>=4
label var ccw_ge4_y`year' "4+ chronic conditions `=`year'-1'-`year'"

}
